<text>It has literally been years since I've had an eye exam, so needless to say I was a little nervous making an appointment. I was able to get an appointment within 5 days of scheduling!  This was my first time going to the Lenscrafters at the Southland Mall. The staff at  the desk were friendly and welcoming. They were very thorough with their paperwork and got me in to do my exam withing a few minutes. I felt very comfortable with the woman that did my exam. Dr. Monica Liou was very kind and took the time to ask me if I had any other questions. This establishment is top notch and I am definitely returning and referring!< /text><date>1483939917725< /date></record>

< Text>
You walk in the door and the first thing they ask you after a polite greeting is whether or not you have money in the parking meter. If not they have a bucket of coins in which you can grab the amount of change you need to put in the meter for the duration of your visit. Then they set a timer to keep you aware of how much time is left on the parking meter. During my visit one of the employees went out and put more change in my meter to ensure I don't get a ticket. They offered water, snacks, and honesty that I have not seen at almost any other business.
Out of many of the coin shops in the valley they had absolutely the best prices, and even rounded down to give me a slight discount on their already discounted prices. I went to another coin dealer
(somewhere on Sepulveda), and they wanted $500 more for the very same item that I got at A Coin Exchange. A Coin Exchange isn't trying to make the most amount of money from each person to stay in business, they use the volume of customers that consistently return. For anybody either wanting to buy or sell precious metals, go to A Coin Exchange<//Text>

< review>
Going to place that you've never visited can be a bit un-nerving but at least having a referral is a little bit of comfort but still the "not-knowing" what to expect fear still lingers. All of that went away as soon as I walked into this place. I was greeted by Pam and soon after was introduced to Jonathan. These are some of the nicest people you could ever want to meet or do business with. Jonathan was so gracious and easy going and carefully went through each and every item I brought to make sure he was giving me the best prices available and Pam was showing me diamonds and custom rings sets that she can create. It was truly a very comfortable transaction and would definitely recommend this place to any and all that would listen. I plan to use Pam for a custom engagement ring in the near future and ANY jewelry or coin business that I may have in the future is coming here. What an absolute joy considering I am the most pesimistic man on the planet!</review>

<Text>I have been having my hair cut by Heidi at West Coast Cuts & Colors for about the last four years.  If she is not there, I will come back another time because I know she knows what I like and does everything she can to make me a happy customer.  Although I know that others may do the same, why chance it when you're happy with a single service provider (of any type), right?

As a guy, I go for the simple wash & cut deal (no desire for coloring, streaking, perms or any of that stuff).  One of the great things is that Heidi knows that I am the type that washes his hair every single day; there's no need to wash my hair before cutting it because it has only been a few hours since the last wash anyway.  Rather than not giving me the wash that is included in the package, she is really nice about washing my hair after the cut.  After all, why should I have all of the little pieces of loose hair falling onto my desk when I go back to work, or even worse, into my food when I have my lunch?

Heidi is always super personable and remembers who you are as a person, not just as a customer.  She makes it a point to ask about things and have real, meaningful, conversations with you while in the chair.  There are some places that you'll go and wish that the stylist would just stop talking because all they do is talk about their own drama but Heidi talks with you as a friend would.  She's also a dog-lover and has two beautiful Miniature Pinschers that we converse about since I have one as well.

I cannot say enough good things about Heidi and the job she does; the prices are reasonable, the cut is always correct (she tracks how to cut your hair within your customer record in the computer), and she treats you right.

What more can you ask for, right?<//Text>< Pics>

We should have made this one of our first stops!  Red Bee has a great atmosphere and you feel it the instant you walk inside the door, greeted by smiling faces and  the waft of delicious coffee, breakfast paninis and pastries this place does not disappoint.

I would highly recommend the chai which I was told they make in house, it has a nice spice and layers of all the different spices. We cant wait for our next trip back!< /review>
